from shared_llm_connector import ask_shared

def chat_with_baby(user_input):
    response = ask_shared(user_input)
    response = response.replace("<think>", "ü§î\\n").replace("</think>", "")
    return response

with gr.Blocks(title="Baby Melah UI") as demo:
    gr.Markdown("## üë∂ ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ - ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢")
    gr.Markdown("‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞ üí¨\\n(‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ ü§î ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏è‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤)")

    chat_history = gr.Chatbot()
    user_input = gr.Textbox(label="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà", placeholder="‡∏™‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏™‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤...", lines=2)
    send_btn = gr.Button("‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°")

    def respond(message, history):
        response = chat_with_baby(message)
        history = history or []
        history.append((message, response))
        return history, ""

    send_btn.click(respond, [user_input, chat_history], [chat_history, user_input])

demo.launch()

def chat_with_baby(user_input):
    response = ask_shared(user_input)
    # ‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤ <think>...</think> ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ regex
    response = re.sub(r"<think>.*?</think>", "ü§î", response, flags=re.DOTALL)
    # ‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô [qwen3:4b]
    response = re.sub(r"^\[.*?\]\s*", "", response)
    return response

# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö LLM (gemma3 ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Localhost)

import requests

def ask_baby(prompt):
    try:
        response = requests.post(
            "http://localhost:11434/api/generate",  # Default Ollama API port
            json={
                "model": "gemma3",  # ‚Üê ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
                "prompt": prompt,
                "stream": False
            }
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        data = response.json()
        return data.get("response", "").strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"[LLM Error]: {str(e)}"

import requests
import json

# ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô endpoint ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô Ollama
LLM_ENDPOINT = "http://localhost:7860/v1/chat/completions"

def chat_with_llm(user_input):
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma3",  # ‚Üê ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢"},
            {"role": "user", "content": user_input}
        ],
        "stream": True  # ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç! ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏•
    }

    with requests.post(LLM_ENDPOINT, headers=headers, json=payload, stream=True) as r:
        partial_response = ""
        for line in r.iter_lines():
            if line:
                try:
                    data = json.loads(line.decode()[6:])
                    delta = data["choices"][0]["delta"].get("content", "")
                    partial_response += delta
                    yield partial_response
                except Exception as e:
                    yield f"‚ö†Ô∏è Error: {e}"

with gr.Blocks() as demo:
    gr.Markdown("## üí¨ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ (Gemma UI ‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏£)")
    chat = gr.Chatbot()
    txt = gr.Textbox(show_label=False, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô '‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞'")
    
    def respond(message, history):
        history = history or []
        full_reply = chat_with_llm(message)
        return full_reply, history + [[message, full_reply]]
    
    txt.submit(respond, [txt, chat], [chat])
    
demo.launch()

def respond(message, history):
    history = history or []
    full_reply = ""

    for delta in chat_with_llm(message):
        full_reply = delta  # ‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°
        yield history + [[message, full_reply]]  # ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö list of list (tuple 2)

    # return history ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏ö
    return history + [[message, full_reply]]

import gradio as gr
import ollama  # ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Ollama

def ask_stream(prompt):
    response = ollama.ChatCompletion.create(
        model="gemma3",  # ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
        messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
        stream=True
    )

    partial = ""
    for chunk in response:
        if "content" in chunk["message"]:
            partial += chunk["message"]["content"]
            yield partial

chatbot = gr.Chatbot()
with gr.Blocks() as demo:
    with gr.Column():
        chatbot_elem = gr.Chatbot()
        user_input = gr.Textbox(placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‚Ä¶", show_label=False)

        def user_respond(message, history):
            return ask_stream(message), history + [[message, ""]]

        user_input.submit(
            fn=user_respond,
            inputs=[user_input, chatbot_elem],
            outputs=[chatbot_elem, chatbot_elem]
        )

demo.launch()

‚úÖ ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ requests + ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏û‡πà‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£
import gradio as gr
import requests
import json

def ask_stream(prompt):
    url = "http://localhost:11434/api/chat"
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    data = {
        "model": "gemma3",  # ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà
        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
        "stream": True
    }

    response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, data=json.dumps(data), stream=True)
    answer = ""
    for line in response.iter_lines():
        if line:
            try:
                json_data = json.loads(line.decode("utf-8"))
                if "message" in json_data and "content" in json_data["message"]:
                    answer += json_data["message"]["content"]
                    yield answer
            except:
                continue

            outputs=[chatbot_elem, chatbot_elem]

‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß (‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà):
import gradio as gr
import requests
import json

def ask_stream(prompt, history):
    url = "http://localhost:11434/api/chat"
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    data = {
        "model": "gemma3",  # ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
        "stream": True
    }

    history = history + [[prompt, ""]]
    response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, data=json.dumps(data), stream=True)

    answer = ""
    for line in response.iter_lines():
        if line:
            try:
                json_data = json.loads(line.decode("utf-8"))
                if "message" in json_data and "content" in json_data["message"]:
                    answer += json_data["message"]["content"]
                    history[-1][1] = answer  # ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
                    yield history
            except:
                continue

chatbot = gr.Chatbot()

with gr.Blocks() as demo:
    chatbot_elem = gr.Chatbot()
    user_input = gr.Textbox(placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‚Ä¶", show_label=False)

    state = gr.State([])

    user_input.submit(
        fn=ask_stream,
        inputs=[user_input, state],
        outputs=[chatbot_elem],
        show_progress=True
    ).then(
        lambda x: "", None, user_input  # ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
    ).then(
        lambda h: h, state, state       # ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö history ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô state
    )

demo.launch()
